He ran after a big gray squirrel that was sitting on a branch. The squirrel saw Spot and was frightened. It jumped from the branch and ran across the pass. The pass was a road with many cars and trucks. It was very noisy and dangerous."Spot, no! The pass is bad! You can get hurt!" Ben shouted.He ran after Spot, but he was too far. He opened his eyes and blinked. He saw Spot on the other side of the pass, wagging his tail. He saw the truck stop and the driver get out. And you saved the squirrel, too. He is not hurt, just scared. I will take him to the vet and then to the woods. He will be happy there."The driver smiled and gave Spot a pat. He agreed. He learned his lesson. He followed Ben back to the park and played with him. They had fun and they were careful. They did not go near the pass again.
